\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__logistic_8py_source_l01698}01698\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ coef\ =\ lr.coef\_.ravel()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__logistic_8py_source_l01699}01699\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ obj\ =\ C\ *\ log\_loss(y,\ lr.predict\_proba(X))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__logistic_8py_source_l01700}01700\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ obj\ +=\ l1\_ratio\ *\ np.sum(np.abs(coef))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__logistic_8py_source_l01701}01701\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ obj\ +=\ (1.0\ -\/\ l1\_ratio)\ *\ 0.5\ *\ np.dot(coef,\ coef)}
